# Best Open Source Alternatives

An awesome list of open source alternatives to proprietary software.

Explore the full directory at [BestAlternative](https://www.bestalternative.dev/?utm_source=github).

## Contents

- [Popular Open Source Alternatives](#popular-open-source-alternatives)
- [All Alternatives](#all-alternatives)
- [About](#about)
